  <script>
   booking.whenReady = (function() {
var queue = [],
isReady = false;
var runner = function (runIfReady, fn, args) {
if (typeof runIfReady === 'function') {
args = fn;
fn = runIfReady;
runIfReady = true;
}
if (isReady) {
runIfReady &amp;&amp; fn.apply(undefined, args || []);
} else {
queue.push({
fn : fn,
args: args || []
});
}
};
runner.ready = function () {
if (!isReady) {
isReady = true;
for (var i = 0, l = queue.length; i &lt; l; i++) {
var it = queue[i];
it.fn.apply(undefined, it.args);
}
queue = null;
}
};
return runner;
})();
booking._onfly.push(function () {
$(document).bind('ready:finished', function() {
setTimeout(booking.whenReady.ready, 4);
});
});
  </script>
  <script>
   booking.clickStore = (function() {
var store = {};
var body = document.body;
if (body &amp;&amp; 'addEventListener' in body) {
body.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
walker(e.target, function (currentTarget) {
var id = currentTarget.getAttribute('data-click-store-id');
if (id) {
store[id] = {
currentTarget: currentTarget,
originalEvent: e
};
}
});
});
}
function walker(el, fn) {
var node = el;
while (node !== null &amp;&amp; node !== body) {
fn(node);
node = node.parentNode;
}
}
function get(el) {
if (el === undefined) {
return store;
} else if (typeof el === 'string') {
var it = store[el];
if (it) {
return it.originalEvent;
}
} else {
var $el = $(el);
var id = $el.attr('data-click-store-id');
var it = store[id];
if (it &amp;&amp; $el.get(0) === it.currentTarget) {
return it.originalEvent;
}
}
}
return {
get : get,
get$: function (el) {
var e = get(el);
return e ? jQuery.Event(e) : e;
}
};
})();
  </script>

         <div class="hp_hotel_description_hightlights_wrapper">
          <div class="hotel_description_wrapper_exp">
           <div class="" id="summary">
            <p>
             This 3-star superior hotel is just 900 yards from Frankfurt am Main Airport Terminal 2. It features a 24-hour reception with live flight information, soundproofed windows, and free Wi-Fi in public areas.
            </p>
            <p>
             The modern rooms at the Meininger Hotel Frankfurt Main/Airport offer a flat-screen TV and an iPod dock. A hairdryer is provided in the private bathroom.
            </p>
            <p>
             Guests can prepare meals in the shared kitchen, and light snacks and drinks can be ordered at the bar.
            </p>
            <p>
             Frankfurt am Main Flughafen Fernbahnhof Train Station is 0.9 miles from the hotel, and the centre of Frankfurt is a 15-minute drive away. The hotel offers a free shuttle service from the airport to the hotel.
            </p>
           </div>
           <p class="summary " style="color: #555; font-size: 95%; font-style: italic; ">
            We speak your language!
Hotel Rooms: 168, 
Hotel Chain:
Meininger Hotels.
This property has been on Booking.com since 4 Nov 2011.
           </p>

        <div class="review_list_outer_container clearfix" id="review_list_score_container">
         <div class="revd_policy revd_collapsible lock_price tr_VXSUbaPQQSRPWdOLXMHO">
          <div class="header">
           <span class="handle hide">
            
           </span>
           <h3 class="headline">
            Why you can trust our reviews
           </h3>
          </div>
          <div class="content" style="display:none;">
           <p>
            Only people who have booked through Booking.com and stayed at the property can write a review. That means our reviews come from real guests, like you.
           </p>
           <p>
            To keep the rating score and review content relevant for your upcoming trip, we archive reviews older than 14 months for properties that have more than 30 reviews.
           </p>
           <a class="no_underline" href="#" id="guidelines_open_link">
            Read more
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <style>
          .guidelines_content {
background: #fff;
padding: 12px 24px;
text-align: justify;
color: #003580;
}
.guidelines_content_lightbox {
background: #fff;
padding: 12px 24px;
text-align: justify;
height: 400px;
overflow-y: scroll;
color: #003580;
}
.guidelines_content p,
.guidelines_content_lightbox p {
margin: 1em 0;
}
.guidelines_content .head,
.guidelines_content_lightbox .head {
font-weight: bold;
font-size: 16px;
}
         </style>
         <title>
          Booking.com guest review guidelines
         </title>
         <div class="guidelines_content_lightbox" id="guidelines_content" style="display:none;">
          <p class="headline">
           Booking.com guest review guidelines
          </p>
          <p>
           Only a customer who has booked through Booking.com and stayed at the property in question can write a review. This lets us know that our reviews come from real guests, like you. Who better to tell others about the free breakfast, friendly staff, or quiet room than someone whos stayed at the property before?
          </p>
          <p>
           We want you to share your story, both the good and the bad. All we ask is that you follow a few simple guidelines.
          </p>
          <p class="head">
           Tips for writing a great review
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Give us details.
           </strong>
           People love to hear about the details. Was the air-conditioning working? Was there a chocolate on your pillow? We like long reviews and suggest you write at least 50 words.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Be candid.
           </strong>
           Give us your honest opinion. Well never remove a review just because its negative. That's our promise to you.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Be relevant.
           </strong>
           The best reviews provide constructive information that helps other travellers to make better choices. Stay on topic and avoid content that others might find offensive.
          </p>
          <p class="head">
           We will sometimes remove reviews if they include the following:
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Objectionable material.
           </strong>
           This includes insulting or discriminatory remarks, swearing or offensive language.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Private information.
           </strong>
           To protect your privacy (and that of others) we do not display reviews that include email addresses or phone numbers.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Sensitive information.
           </strong>
           We do not display reviews that contain information with possible legal implications. This includes references to suspected illegal conduct or allusions to lost or stolen items. In such sensitive cases, you should contact Customer Service, who will be happy to help.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Irrelevant topics.
           </strong>
           This includes promotional content and politically sensitive subjects.
          </p>
          <p class="head">
           In some rare cases, neither the written review nor the review score can be displayed. This only happens when:
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Key information is missing.
           </strong>
           A few review questions are mandatory. If these arent answered, we aren't able to calculate a fair review score, so we can't display the review.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            You didnt stay at the property.
           </strong>
           When necessary, well confirm this information with both you and the accommodation owner.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            You made a mistake.
           </strong>
           Everyone makes mistakes. We wont post yours. If you reviewed a different property from the one you booked, let us know. We can fix it so that your review goes with the right property.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            The review is a fake.
           </strong>
           If there is any indication that a review is not authentic or is in any way fraudulent it will be flagged during the moderation process.
          </p>
         </div>

if (document.getElementById("blockdisplay" + i)) {

if (document.getElementById('blockdisplay' + j)) {
document.getElementById('blockdisplay' + j).style.display = (j === i) ? 'block' : 'none';
}
}
body.trigger((i == 4) ? 'ReviewsTab_onOpen' : 'ReviewsTab_onClose')

.trigger( 'BLOCKDISPLAY' + i + '.OPEN' );

bMovableBookNowButton.init();
}
}
